## Step 0: Scope Challenge

### 1. 已有代码覆盖情况

当前代码库已经实现了规格说明书中**绝大部分功能**：

| 模块   | 已实现                       | 缺失                            |
| ---- | ------------------------- | ----------------------------- |
| 认证   | ✅ 注册/登录/管理员登录/JWT         | ❌ 短信验证码未实际验证、admin\_config表缺失 |
| 餐饮   | ✅ 预约/点餐/换桌/退菜/结账/桌位CRUD   | ❌ 每日库存重置机制                    |
| 产品   | ✅ 产品列表/购买/卡券生成            | ❌ 文件上传接口                      |
| 卡券   | ✅ 查看/转赠/核销/服务预约/取消        | ❌ 无                           |
| 会员   | ✅ 购买/赠送/自动赠送卡券            | ❌ 无                           |
| 种植   | ✅ 地块/摄像头CRUD/服务下单/完成      | ❌ 摄像头队列逻辑(第一期预留)              |
| 日志   | ✅ CRUD/分享/首页展示            | ❌ 无                           |
| 管理后台 | ✅ 仪表盘/用户管理/菜品管理/产品管理/地块管理 | ❌ 无                           |

### 2. 最小变更集

当前项目已处于"功能基本完整"状态，不需要大规模新增。最小变更集是**修复安全和架构问题**，而非增加新功能。

### 3. 复杂度检查

当前代码涉及 **51个Java文件 + 17个Vue页面**，已超过8个文件的复杂度阈值。但这是已有实现，不是新增计划。审查重点应放在**已有代码的质量和安全性**上，而非缩减范围。

### 4. 搜索检查

- Spring Boot 内置验证框架（`spring-boot-starter-validation` 已在 pom.xml 中）→ 当前未使用，应使用 DTO + `@Valid` 替代 `Map<String, Object>`
- MyBatis-Plus 内置乐观锁插件 → 当前未使用，库存扣减存在竞态条件
- Spring Boot 内置 `@Scheduled` → 可用于每日库存重置

### 5. 完整性检查

当前实现存在多处"shortcut"而非完整方案：

- 登录不验证短信验证码（直接放行）
- 库存扣减用 `setSql` 拼接而非乐观锁
- 身份码生成用 `ThreadLocalRandom` 而非数据库唯一约束保障
- 无文件上传接口（图片路径硬编码）

### 6. TODOS 交叉引用

无 `TODOS.md` 文件。

***

**Step 0 结论：** 范围接受为-is。当前项目已实现大部分功能，审查重点放在**安全漏洞、架构缺陷、代码质量、测试覆盖**上。

***

## Section 1: Architecture Review

我发现了以下架构问题，逐个向你确认。

### 架构问题 #1: SQL 注入风险 — `setSql()` 字符串拼接

`[P0] (confidence: 10/10) DiningService.java — 库存扣减使用 setSql 字符串拼接`

在 [DiningService.java](file:///e:/Workspace/AI/Agritainment/server/src/main/java/com/agritainment/service/DiningService.java) 的 `createOrder()` 方法中：

```java
dishMapper.update(null, new LambdaUpdateWrapper<Dish>()
    .eq(Dish::getId, dish.getId())
    .gt(Dish::getRemainingStock, 0)
    .setSql("remaining_stock = remaining_stock - " + item.getQuantity()));
```

`item.getQuantity()` 直接拼入 SQL。虽然 `quantity` 是 `Integer` 类型不太可能注入，但这是不安全的模式。同样的问题存在于 [ProductService.java](file:///e:/Workspace/AI/Agritainment/server/src/main/java/com/agritainment/service/ProductService.java) 的 `purchase()` 方法中。

同时，这种写法在并发场景下存在竞态条件（race condition）：两个请求同时读到 `remaining_stock > 0`，都执行减操作，可能导致库存为负。

D1 决定：**乐观锁 + 原子更新**。后续实现时加 `@Version` 字段 + MyBatis-Plus 乐观锁插件。

***

### 架构问题 #2: 认证体系 — 短信验证码未实际验证

`[P0] (confidence: 10/10) AuthService.java:sendSmsCode() — 空实现，login() 不验证验证码`

```java
public void sendSmsCode(String phone) {
    // 空实现
}

public String login(String phone, String code) {
    // code 参数完全未使用，只要手机号存在就登录成功
    User user = userMapper.selectOne(...);
    if (user == null) throw new AppException(40403, "用户不存在");
    return jwtUtil.generateToken(...);
}
```

任何人知道手机号就能登录。这是严重的安全漏洞。

D2 决定：**内存验证码 + 开发环境固定码 123456**。

***

### 架构问题 #3: 敏感信息硬编码 — application.yml 明文密码和弱 JWT 密钥

`[P1] (confidence: 10/10) application.yml — 数据库密码明文、JWT 密钥过弱`

```yaml
spring:
  datasource:
    username: zhangkun
    password: 138992        # 明文密码
jwt:
  secret: agritainment-secret-key-must-be-at-least-256-bits-long-for-hs256  # 弱密钥
```

JWT 密钥是可预测的字符串，数据库密码直接写在配置文件中。

D3 决定：**暂不处理**，部署时再改。

***

### 架构问题 #4: Controller 层使用 Map\<String, Object> 而非 DTO

`[P1] (confidence: 9/10) 所有 Controller — 用 Map 接收请求体，无类型安全和验证`

所有 Controller 的 `@RequestBody` 都是 `Map<String, Object>`，然后手动 `.get()` + `.toString()` + 类型转换。问题：

- 无编译期类型检查
- 无参数验证（`@NotBlank`, `@NotNull` 等注解无法使用）
- 字段名拼错不会报错，运行时 NPE
- `pom.xml` 已引入 `spring-boot-starter-validation` 但完全未使用

D4 决定：**全量 DTO + @Valid**。

***

### 架构问题 #5: CORS 配置过于宽松

`[P2] (confidence: 9/10) WebConfig.java — allowedOriginPatterns("*") + allowCredentials(true)`

```java
registry.addMapping("/api/v1/**")
    .allowedOriginPatterns("*")
    .allowedMethods("GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE")
    .allowedHeaders("*")
    .allowCredentials(true);
```

允许任何来源携带凭证访问 API。生产环境应限制为小程序域名。

D5 决定：**Profile 区分环境**。

***

### 架构问题 #6: 缺少文件上传接口

`[P2] (confidence: 8/10) 整个后端 — 无文件上传 API`

菜品图片、产品图片、用户头像、日志图片都引用了路径（如 `/images/dishes/chicken.jpg`），但后端没有任何上传接口。前端也没有上传功能。

D6 决定：**添加本地文件上传接口**。

***

### 架构问题 #7: 每日库存/配额无重置机制

`[P2] (confidence: 9/10) Dish.remainingStock / Product.remainingQuota — 无每日重置`

`data.sql` 中菜品和产品都有初始库存，但用完就没了。没有定时任务在每天零点将 `remaining_stock` 重置为 `daily_stock`，将 `remaining_quota` 重置为 `daily_quota`。

D7 决定：**暂不处理**，后续加。

***

### 架构问题 #8: 前端 API 层重复方法

`[P2] (confidence: 8/10) api/index.js — adminApi 重复了 diningApi 和 plantingApi 的方法`

```js
// adminApi 中重复：
getAllTables: () => get('/dining/all-tables'),    // = diningApi.getAllTables
createTable: (data) => post('/dining/tables', data), // = diningApi.createTable
deleteTable: (id) => del(`/dining/tables/${id}`),    // = diningApi.deleteTable
getCameras: () => get('/planting/cameras'),           // = plantingApi.getCameras
// ...

// productApi 中重复：
getList: () => get('/products'),    // = getProducts
```

D8 决定：**去重，admin 复用其他模块**。

***

架构审查完成，共 8 个问题。进入代码质量审查。

***

## Section 2: Code Quality Review

### 代码质量问题 #1: DRY 违规 — checkNoShow() 重复实现

`[P1] (confidence: 10/10) DiningService.java + PlantingService.java — 爽约检查逻辑完全重复`

两个 Service 都有完全相同的 `checkNoShow()` 方法：

```java
private boolean checkNoShow(Long userId, LocalDateTime reservationTime) {
    long hoursDiff = java.time.Duration.between(LocalDateTime.now(), reservationTime).toHours();
    if (hoursDiff < 6) {
        User user = userMapper.selectById(userId);
        int newCount = (user.getNoShowCount() != null ? user.getNoShowCount() : 0) + 1;
        userMapper.update(null, new LambdaUpdateWrapper<User>().eq(User::getId, userId)
                .set(User::getNoShowCount, newCount).set(User::getIsBlacklisted, newCount >= 3));
        return true;
    }
    return false;
}
```

同样，`generateCode()` 在 AuthService、ProductService、PlantingService 中重复了 3 次。

D9 决定：**提取到 UserService**。

***

### 代码质量问题 #2: 错误处理 — MembershipService 赠送卡券异常被静默吞掉

`[P1] (confidence: 10/10) MembershipService.java:purchase() — catch (Exception ignored) {}`

```java
if (config.getGiftProductIds() != null) {
    try {
        var mapper = new com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper();
        var productIds = mapper.readValue(config.getGiftProductIds(), java.util.List.class);
        for (Object pid : productIds) {
            // ... 创建赠送卡券
        }
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
        // 静默吞掉异常！
    }
}
```

如果赠送卡券创建失败（JSON 解析错误、数据库写入失败），用户付了会员费但没收到赠送卡券，且无任何日志或错误提示。

D10 决定：**异常回滚事务**。

***

### 代码质量问题 #3: 身份码生成存在碰撞风险

`[P2] (confidence: 7/10) AuthService/ProductService/PlantingService — ThreadLocalRandom 生成 12 位码无重试`

```java
private String generateCode() {
    return String.valueOf(100000000000L + ThreadLocalRandom.current().nextLong(900000000000L));
}
```

虽然 12 位数字空间很大（9000亿），碰撞概率低，但数据库有 `UNIQUE` 约束，碰撞时 insert 会直接抛异常而非友好重试。

D11 决定：**碰撞重试**。

***

### 代码质量问题 #4: 前端请求层缺少错误处理

`[P2] (confidence: 8/10) api/request.js — 未读取到内容，但从 api/index.js 推断缺少统一错误处理`

前端 API 层封装了 `get/post/del/put`，但根据 auth store 的用法（直接 `await authApi.login()` 取 data），推断 request.js 没有统一处理：

- 401 未登录自动跳转登录页
- 网络错误提示
- Token 过期自动刷新或跳转

D12 决定：**加统一错误拦截**。

***

### 代码质量问题 #5: GlobalExceptionHandler 吞掉异常堆栈

`[P2] (confidence: 8/10) GlobalExceptionHandler.java — 通用异常只 e.printStackTrace()`

```java
@ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
public Result<?> handleException(Exception e) {
    e.printStackTrace();  // 只打印到 stderr，无结构化日志
    return Result.error(50000, "服务器内部错误");
}
```

`e.printStackTrace()` 在生产环境中不可靠（可能丢失、不按顺序），应使用 SLF4J/Logback 结构化日志。

D13 决定：**改用 SLF4J 日志**。

***

### 代码质量问题 #6: 桌位预约状态管理缺陷

`[P2] (confidence: 8/10) DiningService.java:getTables() — 用修改 qrCode 字段标记预约状态`

```java
tables.forEach(t -> {
    t.setQrCode(reservedTableIds.contains(t.getId()) ? "RESERVED" : t.getQrCode());
});
```

把桌位的 `qrCode`（二维码标识）临时改成 `"RESERVED"` 来标记已被预约。这破坏了数据完整性——前端拿到 `"RESERVED"` 作为 qrCode 无法用于扫码点餐。

D14 决定：**返回独立预约状态字段**。

***

代码质量审查完成，共 6 个问题。进入测试审查。

***

`pom.xml` 已包含 `spring-boot-starter-test`（JUnit 5 + Mockito），但 **src/test/ 目录下没有任何测试文件**。前端也没有任何测试配置。


### 关键缺失测试

| 优先级          | 测试          | 原因                                          |
| ------------ | ----------- | ------------------------------------------- |
| **CRITICAL** | 爽约+黑名单逻辑    | 3次爽约自动黑名单，业务核心规则                            |
| **CRITICAL** | 库存扣减竞态      | 并发下单可能导致超卖                                  |
| **CRITICAL** | 卡券状态流转      | available→locked→used/available，错误流转导致数据不一致 |
| **HIGH**     | 会员购买+赠送卡券事务 | 付费后赠送失败需回滚                                  |
| **HIGH**     | 认证流程        | 注册/登录/管理员登录                                 |
| **HIGH**     | 预约取消6小时规则   | 爽约计数的核心判断                                   |
| **MEDIUM**   | 换桌/退菜       | 金额重算正确性                                     |
| **MEDIUM**   | 转赠卡券        | 新码生成+所有权转移                                  |

D15 决定：**关键路径单元测试**（爽约黑名单、库存竞态、卡券状态流转）。

***

测试审查完成。进入性能审查。

***

## Section 4: Performance Review

### 性能问题 #1: N+1 查询 — 订单创建循环中逐个查询菜品

`[P1] (confidence: 9/10) DiningService.java:createOrder() — 循环内 selectById + update`

```java
for (OrderItem item : items) {
    Dish dish = dishMapper.selectById(item.getDishId());  // N 次查询
    // ...
    dishMapper.update(null, ...);  // N 次更新
    orderItemMapper.insert(oi);    // N 次插入
}
```

一次下单 N 个菜品 = 3N 次数据库操作。应批量查询菜品、批量插入订单项。

### 性能问题 #2: Dashboard 多次 COUNT 查询

`[P2] (confidence: 7/10) AdminService.java:getDashboard() — 7 次 COUNT 查询`

```java
data.put("customerCount", userMapper.selectCount(...));
data.put("staffCount", userMapper.selectCount(...));
data.put("memberCount", userMapper.selectCount(...));
data.put("tableCount", tableMapper.selectCount(null));
data.put("productCount", productMapper.selectCount(null));
data.put("plotCount", plotMapper.selectCount(null));
data.put("rentedPlotCount", plotMapper.selectCount(...));
```

7 次独立 COUNT 查询。可合并为 1-2 条 SQL。

### 性能问题 #3: 前端无开发代理配置

`[P2] (confidence: 8/10) vite.config.js — 无 proxy 配置`

开发时前端请求 `localhost:8080` 需要跨域，目前靠后端 CORS 解决。但小程序端不支持 CORS，开发体验差。

D16 决定：**修复 N+1 + 代理**。

### Worktree parallelization strategy

本次修复涉及多个独立模块，可并行：

| Lane  | 步骤                  | 模块                                     |
| ----- | ------------------- | -------------------------------------- |
| **A** | DTO重构 + @Valid      | controller/, dto/ (新建)                 |
| **B** | 安全修复 (乐观锁+验证码+CORS) | service/, config/, entity/             |
| **C** | 前端修复 (去重+错误拦截+代理)   | client/src/api/, client/vite.config.js |
| **D** | 测试编写                | test/ (新建)                             |

执行顺序：**A + B 并行 → C 独立 → D 最后**（测试依赖代码稳定）

## 1. CouponController.java

Path: `e:\Workspace\AI\Agritainment\server\src\main\java\com\agritainment\controller\CouponController.java`

```java
package com.agritainment.controller;

import com.agritainment.annotation.RequireRole;
import com.agritainment.common.Result;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateServiceReservationRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.TransferCouponRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.VerifyCouponRequest;
import com.agritainment.entity.Coupon;
import com.agritainment.entity.ServiceReservation;
import com.agritainment.service.CouponService;
import com.agritainment.service.ProductService;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.util.List;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/coupons")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class CouponController {

    private final CouponService couponService;
    private final ProductService productService;

    @GetMapping
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<List<Coupon>> getCoupons(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId) {
        return Result.ok(couponService.getCoupons(userId));
    }

    @GetMapping("/{id}")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Coupon> getCoupon(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId, @PathVariable Long id) {
        return Result.ok(couponService.getCoupon(userId, id));
    }

    @PostMapping("/{id}/transfer")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Coupon> transfer(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @PathVariable Long id,
            @Valid @RequestBody TransferCouponRequest request) {
        return Result.ok(couponService.transfer(userId, id, request.getTarget_user_id()));
    }

    @PostMapping("/verify")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Coupon> verifyCoupon(@Valid @RequestBody VerifyCouponRequest request) {
        return Result.ok(productService.verifyCoupon(request.getCode()));
    }

    @PostMapping("/service-reservations")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<ServiceReservation> createServiceReservation(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @Valid @RequestBody CreateServiceReservationRequest request) {
        return Result.ok(couponService.createServiceReservation(userId, request.getCoupon_id(), request.getProduct_id(), request.getDate()));
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/service-reservations/{id}")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> cancelServiceReservation(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @PathVariable Long id) {
        couponService.cancelServiceReservation(userId, id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }
}
```

Changes:

- Removed `java.time.LocalDate` and `java.util.Map` imports (no longer needed)
- Added `com.agritainment.dto.TransferCouponRequest`, `com.agritainment.dto.VerifyCouponRequest`, `com.agritainment.dto.CreateServiceReservationRequest` imports
- Added `jakarta.validation.Valid` import
- `transfer()`: `Map<String, Object> body` replaced with `@Valid @RequestBody TransferCouponRequest request`, uses `request.getTarget_user_id()`
- `verifyCoupon()`: `Map<String, String> body` replaced with `@Valid @RequestBody VerifyCouponRequest request`, uses `request.getCode()`
- `createServiceReservation()`: `Map<String, Object> body` replaced with `@Valid @RequestBody CreateServiceReservationRequest request`, uses `request.getCoupon_id()`, `request.getProduct_id()`, `request.getDate()`

***

## 2. JournalController.java

Path: `e:\Workspace\AI\Agritainment\server\src\main\java\com\agritainment\controller\JournalController.java`

```java
package com.agritainment.controller;

import com.agritainment.annotation.RequireRole;
import com.agritainment.common.Result;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateJournalRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.UpdateJournalRequest;
import com.agritainment.entity.Journal;
import com.agritainment.service.JournalService;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.util.List;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/journals")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class JournalController {

    private final JournalService journalService;

    @GetMapping
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<List<Journal>> getJournals(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId) {
        return Result.ok(journalService.getJournals(userId));
    }

    @GetMapping("/shared")
    public Result<List<Journal>> getSharedJournals() {
        return Result.ok(journalService.getSharedJournals());
    }

    @PostMapping
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Journal> createJournal(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @Valid @RequestBody CreateJournalRequest request) {
        return Result.ok(journalService.createJournal(userId, request.getTitle(), request.getContent(), request.getImages()));
    }

    @PutMapping("/{id}")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Journal> updateJournal(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @PathVariable Long id,
            @Valid @RequestBody UpdateJournalRequest request) {
        return Result.ok(journalService.updateJournal(userId, id, request.getTitle(), request.getContent(), request.getImages()));
    }

    @PostMapping("/{id}/share")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> shareJournal(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId, @PathVariable Long id) {
        journalService.shareJournal(userId, id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/{id}/share")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> unshareJournal(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId, @PathVariable Long id) {
        journalService.unshareJournal(userId, id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }
}
```

Changes:

- Removed `java.util.Map` import
- Added `com.agritainment.dto.CreateJournalRequest`, `com.agritainment.dto.UpdateJournalRequest` imports
- Added `jakarta.validation.Valid` import
- `createJournal()`: `Map<String, Object> body` replaced with `@Valid @RequestBody CreateJournalRequest request`, uses `request.getTitle()`, `request.getContent()`, `request.getImages()`
- `updateJournal()`: `Map<String, Object> body` replaced with `@Valid @RequestBody UpdateJournalRequest request`, uses `request.getTitle()`, `request.getContent()`, `request.getImages()`

***

```java
package com.agritainment.controller;

import com.agritainment.annotation.RequireRole;
import com.agritainment.common.Result;
import com.agritainment.dto.GrantMembershipRequest;
import com.agritainment.entity.MembershipConfig;
import com.agritainment.service.MembershipService;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.util.Map;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/membership")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class MembershipController {

    private final MembershipService membershipService;

    @GetMapping("/status")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Map<String, Object>> getStatus(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId) {
        return Result.ok(membershipService.getStatus(userId));
    }

    @PostMapping("/purchase")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Map<String, Object>> purchase(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId) {
        return Result.ok(membershipService.purchase(userId));
    }

    @GetMapping("/config")
    public Result<MembershipConfig> getConfig() {
        return Result.ok(membershipService.getConfig());
    }

    @PostMapping("/grant")
    @RequireRole({"admin"})
    public Result<Void> grant(@Valid @RequestBody GrantMembershipRequest request) {
        membershipService.grant(request.getUser_id());
        return Result.ok(null);
    }
}
```

Changes:

- Kept `java.util.Map` import (still used for return types in `getStatus()` and `purchase()`)
- Added `com.agritainment.dto.GrantMembershipRequest` import
- Added `jakarta.validation.Valid` import
- `grant()`: `Map<String, Object> body` replaced with `@Valid @RequestBody GrantMembershipRequest request`, uses `request.getUser_id()`

## 4. PlantingController.java

Path: `e:\Workspace\AI\Agritainment\server\src\main\java\com\agritainment\controller\PlantingController.java`

```java
package com.agritainment.controller;

import com.agritainment.annotation.RequireRole;
import com.agritainment.common.Result;
import com.agritainment.dto.ControlCameraRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateCameraRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateServiceOrderRequest;
import com.agritainment.entity.Camera;
import com.agritainment.entity.GardenService;
import com.agritainment.entity.GardenServiceOrder;
import com.agritainment.entity.Plot;
import com.agritainment.service.PlantingService;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/planting")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class PlantingController {

    private final PlantingService plantingService;

    @GetMapping("/plots")
    public Result<List<Plot>> getPlots() {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.getPlots());
    }

    @PostMapping("/plots/{id}/rent")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Plot> rentPlot(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId, @PathVariable Long id) {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.rentPlot(userId, id));
    }

    @GetMapping("/garden-services")
    public Result<List<GardenService>> getGardenServices() {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.getGardenServices());
    }

    @PostMapping("/service-orders")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<GardenServiceOrder> createServiceOrder(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @Valid @RequestBody CreateServiceOrderRequest request) {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.createServiceOrder(userId, request.getPlot_id(), request.getService_id(), request.getCoupon_id()));
    }

    @GetMapping("/cameras/{id}/status")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Map<String, Object>> getCameraStatus(@PathVariable Long id) {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.getCameraStatus(id));
    }

    @PostMapping("/cameras/{id}/control")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Map<String, Object>> controlCamera(
            @PathVariable Long id,
            @Valid @RequestBody ControlCameraRequest request) {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.controlCamera(id, request.getAction(), request.getSpeed()));
    }

    @PostMapping("/service-orders/{id}/complete")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<GardenServiceOrder> completeServiceOrder(
            @PathVariable Long id,
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long staffId) {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.completeServiceOrder(id, staffId));
    }

    @GetMapping("/cameras")
    @RequireRole({"admin"})
    public Result<List<Camera>> getCameras() {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.getCameras());
    }

    @PostMapping("/cameras")
    @RequireRole({"admin"})
    public Result<Camera> createCamera(@Valid @RequestBody CreateCameraRequest request) {
        return Result.ok(plantingService.createCamera(
                request.getIdentifier(),
                request.getName(),
                request.getIp_address()));
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/cameras/{id}")
    @RequireRole({"admin"})
    public Result<Void> deleteCamera(@PathVariable Long id) {
        plantingService.deleteCamera(id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }

    @PostMapping("/cameras/{cameraId}/bind-plot/{plotId}")
    @RequireRole({"admin"})
    public Result<Void> bindCameraPlot(@PathVariable Long cameraId, @PathVariable Long plotId) {
        plantingService.bindCameraPlot(cameraId, plotId);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }
}
```

```java
        adminService.deleteDish(id);
        return Result.ok(null);

        return Result.ok(adminService.createProduct(
                request.getName(),

                request.getMember_price(),

        return Result.ok(adminService.updateProduct(id,
```

```java
package com.agritainment.controller;

import com.agritainment.annotation.RequireRole;
import com.agritainment.common.Result;
import com.agritainment.dto.ChangeTableRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateOrderRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateReservationRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateTableRequest;
import com.agritainment.entity.*;
import com.agritainment.service.DiningService;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.format.annotation.DateTimeFormat;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/dining")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class DiningController {

    private final DiningService diningService;

    @GetMapping("/tables")
    public Result<List<Map<String, Object>>> getTables(
            @RequestParam(required = false) @DateTimeFormat(iso = DateTimeFormat.ISO.DATE) LocalDate date,
            @RequestParam(required = false) String time_slot) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.getTables(date, time_slot));
    }

    @PostMapping("/reservations")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<TableReservation> createReservation(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @RequestBody @Valid CreateReservationRequest req) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.createReservation(userId, req.getTable_id(), req.getDate(), req.getTime_slot()));
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/reservations/{id}")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<TableReservation> cancelReservation(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @PathVariable Long id) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.cancelReservation(userId, id));
    }

    @GetMapping("/reservations")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<List<TableReservation>> getReservations(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.getReservations(userId));
    }

    @GetMapping("/orders/active")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Object> getActiveOrder(@RequestParam(required = false) String table_qr) {
        if (table_qr != null) {
            return Result.ok(diningService.getActiveOrder(table_qr));
        }
        return Result.ok(diningService.getActiveOrders());
    }

    @PostMapping("/orders")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Order> createOrder(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @RequestBody @Valid CreateOrderRequest req) {
        List<OrderItem> items = req.getItems().stream().map(input -> {
            OrderItem item = new OrderItem();
            item.setDishId(input.getDish_id());
            item.setQuantity(input.getQuantity());
            return item;
        }).collect(Collectors.toList());
        return Result.ok(diningService.createOrder(userId, req.getTable_qr(), items));
    }

    @PostMapping("/orders/{id}/settle")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Order> settleOrder(@PathVariable Long id) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.settleOrder(id));
    }

    @GetMapping("/dishes")
    public Result<List<Dish>> getDishes() {
        return Result.ok(diningService.getDishes());
    }

    @PostMapping("/staff/reservations/{id}/checkin")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> staffCheckin(@PathVariable Long id) {
        diningService.staffCheckin(id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }

    @PostMapping("/staff/reservations/{id}/cancel")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> staffCancel(@PathVariable Long id) {
        diningService.staffCancelReservation(id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }

    @PostMapping("/orders/{id}/change-table")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> changeTable(@PathVariable Long id, @RequestBody @Valid ChangeTableRequest req) {
        diningService.changeTable(id, req.getNew_table_id());
        return Result.ok(null);
    }

    @PostMapping("/order-items/{id}/refund")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> refundOrderItem(@PathVariable Long id) {
        diningService.refundOrderItem(id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }

    @GetMapping("/all-tables")
    @RequireRole({"admin"})
    public Result<List<DiningTable>> getAllTables() {
        return Result.ok(diningService.getAllTables());
    }

    @PostMapping("/tables")
    @RequireRole({"admin"})
    public Result<DiningTable> createTable(@RequestBody @Valid CreateTableRequest req) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.createTable(req.getTable_number(), req.getCapacity()));
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/tables/{id}")
    @RequireRole({"admin"})
    public Result<Void> deleteTable(@PathVariable Long id) {
        diningService.deleteTable(id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }
}
```

```java
package com.agritainment.controller;

import com.agritainment.annotation.RequireRole;
import com.agritainment.common.Result;
import com.agritainment.dto.ChangeTableRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateOrderRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateReservationRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.CreateTableRequest;
import com.agritainment.entity.*;
import com.agritainment.service.DiningService;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.format.annotation.DateTimeFormat;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/dining")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class DiningController {

    private final DiningService diningService;

    @GetMapping("/tables")
    public Result<List<Map<String, Object>>> getTables(
            @RequestParam(required = false) @DateTimeFormat(iso = DateTimeFormat.ISO.DATE) LocalDate date,
            @RequestParam(required = false) String time_slot) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.getTables(date, time_slot));
    }

    @PostMapping("/reservations")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<TableReservation> createReservation(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @RequestBody @Valid CreateReservationRequest req) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.createReservation(userId, req.getTable_id(), req.getDate(), req.getTime_slot()));
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/reservations/{id}")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<TableReservation> cancelReservation(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @PathVariable Long id) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.cancelReservation(userId, id));
    }

    @GetMapping("/reservations")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<List<TableReservation>> getReservations(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.getReservations(userId));
    }

    @GetMapping("/orders/active")
    @RequireRole({"customer", "staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Object> getActiveOrder(@RequestParam(required = false) String table_qr) {
        if (table_qr != null) {
            return Result.ok(diningService.getActiveOrder(table_qr));
        }
        return Result.ok(diningService.getActiveOrders());
    }

    @PostMapping("/orders")

    public Result<Order> createOrder(
            @RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId,
            @RequestBody @Valid CreateOrderRequest req) {
        List<OrderItem> items = req.getItems().stream().map(input -> {
            OrderItem item = new OrderItem();
            item.setDishId(input.getDish_id());
            item.setQuantity(input.getQuantity());
            return item;
        }).collect(Collectors.toList());
        return Result.ok(diningService.createOrder(userId, req.getTable_qr(), items));

    @PostMapping("/orders/{id}/settle")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Order> settleOrder(@PathVariable Long id) {
        return Result.ok(diningService.settleOrder(id));
    }

    @GetMapping("/dishes")
    public Result<List<Dish>> getDishes() {
        return Result.ok(diningService.getDishes());
    }

    @PostMapping("/staff/reservations/{id}/checkin")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> staffCheckin(@PathVariable Long id) {
        diningService.staffCheckin(id);
        return Result.ok(null);
    }

    @PostMapping("/staff/reservations/{id}/cancel")
    @RequireRole({"staff", "admin"})
    public Result<Void> staffCancel(@PathVariable Long id) {
        diningService.staffCancelReservation(id);
        return Result.ok(null);

    @PostMapping("/orders/{id}/change-table")

```

对 [DiningController.java](file:///e:/Workspace/AI/Agritainment/server/src/main/java/com/agritainment/controller/DiningController.java) 所做的更改摘要：

1. **移除了导入**：`com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference` 和 `com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper` —— 不再需要，因为 DTO 替换了手动 JSON 转换。
2. **添加了导入**：
   - `com.agritainment.dto.ChangeTableRequest`
   - `com.agritainment.dto.CreateOrderRequest`
   - `com.agritainment.dto.CreateReservationRequest`
   - `com.agritainment.dto.CreateTableRequest`
   - `jakarta.validation.Valid`
   - `java.util.stream.Collectors`
3. **移除了字段**：`private final ObjectMapper objectMapper` —— 不再注入，因为 `ObjectMapper` 不再使用。
4. **`getTables`** **返回类型更改**：从 `Result<List<DiningTable>>` 到 `Result<List<Map<String, Object>>>`，以匹配更新的服务方法签名。
5. **`createReservation`**：将 `@RequestBody Map<String, Object> body` 替换为 `@RequestBody @Valid CreateReservationRequest req`，并使用 `req.getTable_id()`、`req.getDate()`、`req.getTime_slot()`，而不是手动映射提取。
6. **`createOrder`**：将 `@RequestBody Map<String, Object> body` 替换为 `@RequestBody @Valid CreateOrderRequest req`。添加了流式转换，将 `CreateOrderRequest.OrderItemInput`（字段：`dish_id`、`quantity`）映射到实体 `OrderItem`（字段：`dishId`、`quantity`），替换了 `objectMapper.convertValue()` 调用。
7. **`changeTable`**：将 `@RequestBody Map<String, Object> body` 替换为 `@RequestBody @Valid ChangeTableRequest req`，并使用 `req.getNew_table_id()` 而不是 `body.get("new_table_id")`。
8. **`createTable`**：将 `@RequestBody Map<String, Object> body` 替换为 `@RequestBody @Valid CreateTableRequest req`，并使用 `req.getTable_number()` 和 `req.getCapacity()`，而不是手动映射提取及空值检查。
9. **移除了所有注释**，按照要求。

All three DTOs exist. Now writing the rewritten `AuthController.java`:

```java
package com.agritainment.controller;

import com.agritainment.common.Result;
import com.agritainment.dto.AdminLoginRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.LoginRequest;
import com.agritainment.dto.SmsCodeRequest;
import com.agritainment.entity.User;
import com.agritainment.service.AuthService;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.util.Map;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/auth")
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class AuthController {

    private final AuthService authService;

    @PostMapping("/sms-code")
    public Result<Void> sendSmsCode(@Valid @RequestBody SmsCodeRequest req) {
        authService.sendSmsCode(req.getPhone());
        return Result.ok(null);
    }

    @PostMapping("/register")
    public Result<Map<String, String>> register(@Valid @RequestBody LoginRequest req) {
        String token = authService.register(req.getPhone(), req.getCode());
        return Result.ok(Map.of("token", token));
    }

    @PostMapping("/login")
    public Result<Map<String, String>> login(@Valid @RequestBody LoginRequest req) {
        String token = authService.login(req.getPhone(), req.getCode());
        return Result.ok(Map.of("token", token));
    }

    @PostMapping("/admin-login")
    public Result<Map<String, String>> adminLogin(@Valid @RequestBody AdminLoginRequest req) {
        String token = authService.adminLogin(req.getPhone(), req.getPassword());
        return Result.ok(Map.of("token", token));
    }

    @GetMapping("/me")
    public Result<User> getMe(@RequestAttribute("userId") Long userId) {
        return Result.ok(authService.getUserInfo(userId));
    }
}
```

The file has been rewritten with the following changes:

1. **Replaced** **`Map<String, String>`** **parameters with typed DTOs +** **`@Valid`**:
   - `sendSmsCode` now uses `@Valid @RequestBody SmsCodeRequest req` (phone field)
   - `register` now uses `@Valid @RequestBody LoginRequest req` (phone + code fields)
   - `login` now uses `@Valid @RequestBody LoginRequest req` (phone + code fields)
   - `adminLogin` now uses `@Valid @RequestBody AdminLoginRequest req` (phone + password fields)
2. **Replaced** **`body.get(...)`** **calls with getter methods**: `req.getPhone()`, `req.getCode()`, `req.getPassword()`
3. **Updated imports**:
   - Added `com.agritainment.dto.AdminLoginRequest`, `com.agritainment.dto.LoginRequest`, `com.agritainment.dto.SmsCodeRequest`
   - Added `jakarta.validation.Valid`
   - Removed unused `com.agritainment.annotation.RequireRole`
   - Kept `java.util.Map` (still needed for `Map.of("token", token)` return values)
4. **No comments** added, as requested.
